1a1(rgyud): @#/ /rgyud nga pa bzhugs so//
1b1(rgyud): @##/ /rgya gar skad du/ a nA bi la tan+t+ra rA dzA nA ma/ bod skad du /rgyud kyi
1b2(rgyud): rgyal po rnyog pa med pa zhes bya ba/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sems
1b3(rgyud): can rnams la phan 'dod pas/ /rnyog med rab tu bshad par bya/ /snang ba med
1b4(rgyud): cing dpe med pa/ /tshig gi yul las rnam par 'das/ /zhi zhing bdag med
2a1(rgyud): @##/ /dag pa nyid/ /mtshan med mtshan gzhi rnam par spangs/ /ngang gis sangs rgyas
2a2(rgyud): 'di nyid tshul/ /mtshan med mtshan gzhi rnam par spangs/ /khyad par du yang mdor bsdus pas/ /
2a3(rgyud): bdag gis gsal bar bshad pa yin/ /rmongs pa rnams la phan 'dod pas/ /snying rjes 'di ni
2a4(rgyud): bstan pa yin/ /kha cig stong par 'dod pa dang / /kha cig thig le'i gzugs can dang / /kha cig
2a5(rgyud): khyab 'jug tshul gyis ni/ /blo dman dag ni 'jog par byed/ /de nyid nges par yang dag par/ /rgyu
2b1(rgyud): yi gnas kyi spyod yul nyid/ /rgyu dang 'bras bum grub na/ /bsgoms pa med cing byang chub med/ /rgyu yi yid ches spangs
2b2(rgyud): pa 'di/ /thog ma tha ma med pa'i bdag /sgyu ma'i ye shes las byung ba/ /rnam pa sna tshogs ston par byed/ /kha cig
2b3(rgyud): drag po'i rang bzhin du/ /kha cig zhi ba chen po che/ /kha cig phyag rgya'i rang bzhin gzugs/ /kha cig 'dar zhing
2b4(rgyud): g.yo ba dang / /glu gar de bzhin sil snyan dang / /lha yi sngags ni brjod pa nyid/ /kha cig sngags ni yang dag
2b5(rgyud): dgod/ /kha cig dkyil 'khor bri ba dang / /dbang la sogs pa brtag pa dang / /'byung dang 'byung las gyur pa'i
2b6(rgyud): lus| |de ltar la sogs mtha' yas mchog / sangs rgyas la sogs rdo rje brtags/ /gang tshe sems ni legs
3a1(rgyud): @##/ /gnas pa/ /de bzhin nyid kyi spyod yul nyid/ /dkyil 'khor de bzhin 'gyur ba ni/ /phan 'dod rnams
3a2(rgyud): kyis shes par bya/ /phung po la sogs tshogs rnams kyis/ /gang zhig khyad par gyis bcos pa/ /lus ngag yid gsum
3a3(rgyud): bcos pa'i phyir/ /rdul tshon dkyil 'khor zhes bya ra gsungs/ /phung sogs gzhan sogs mthong ba'i phyir/ /tshogs kyi
3a4(rgyud): dkyil 'khor zhes byar gsungs/ /sems kyi dkyil 'khor dag pa ste/ /rang bzhin med par bsgom par bya/ /me long lta
3a5(rgyud): bu gcig nyid de/ /dang po grwar ni rtogs par bya/ /so sor rtog pa zhes gsungs pas/ /shar gyi grwar ni rnam par brgyan//
3a6(rgyud): bya ba nan tan khyad 'phags pa/ /byang gi grwar ni rnam par spros/ /mnyam nyid ye shes chen po ni/ /bag chags med grwa
3b1(rgyud): rjes rtogs byed/ /gzhan du'ang dkyil 'khor gru bzhi pa/ /grwa yi dbus ni thams cad du/ /de nyid 'di ni rab 'jug pas/ /ye shes spyod yul du ni brtag /sgo bzhir yang
3b2(rgyud): dag brjod pa ni/ /de bzhin dran pa bzhir byung ba/ /de bzhin grwa bzhir gsungs pa ni/ /sbyin pa bzhi ni rnam dge ba/ /dbus su dkyil 'khor gzugs su ni/ /mi bskyod pa
3b3(rgyud): yis rnam par brgyan/ /zhi dang chos don brgyan pa las/ /de dag thams cad dkyil 'khor 'grub/ /dra ba dra phyed zla ba sogs/ /dkyil 'khor du ni bris pa dang / /rta babs la
3b4(rgyud): sogs thams cad ni/ /ting 'dzin yan lag rta babs nyid/ /sems kyi mthar thug brjod pa ste/ /de nyid rang bzhin las ni gsungs/ /gang zhig sems kyi rab 'phel ba/ /
3b5(rgyud): ting 'dzin yan lag rnam par gnas/ /de nyid dra ba zhes su gsungs/ /dra ba phyed pa phyed du ste/ /dril bu do shal brtag pa ni/ /rang gi btsun mo rtogs par byed/ /sgra brnyan rnam
3b6(rgyud): pa lta bur ni/ /chos rnams thams cad so sor rtogs/ /chos rnams ma skyes mthong ba'i phyir/ /de nyid rgyal mtshan phreng bar gsungs/ /bla re la sogs gang bres pa/ /
3b7(rgyud): dngos po la sogs dang por nges/ /sems ni bla re zhes byar bshad/ /dam pa'i don las gsungs pa'o/ /gos phreng de dag thams cad ni/ /rnam pa sna tshogs snang ba nyid/ /
4a1(rgyud): @#/ /gang zhig rdo rje rnam pa'i sems/ /dga' ba'i ye shes kyis ni mtshan/ /de yi 'og tu rtag tu gsungs/ /grwa yi mtshams ni thams cad du/ /
4a2(rgyud): rdo rje rin chen rtogs pa'i phyir/ /rdo rje rin po che yis spras/ /zla ba nyi ma gang gsungs pa/ /thabs dang shes rab don mthong phyir/ /thabs dang shes rab bdag nyid sems//
4a3(rgyud): ye shes 'dis ni rnam par brgyan/ /sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje skyes/ /de nyid dkyil 'khor du ni gsungs/ /sku gsungs thugs ni nye ba'i phyir/ /rnam pa gcig tu mtshan nyid med
4a4(rgyud): bla ma slob ma rnams gsal bar/ /rab tu 'jug pa de nyid gsungs/ /sbyin sreg yang ni bshad pa yang / /lha rnams tshim pa nga yis brjod/ /rnam rtog med pa'i sems gang
4a5(rgyud): ni| |thab khung sgra yis mtshan pa nyid/ /bye brag phyed pas me nang du/ /gzugs kyi phung sogs lnga po rnams/ /sems las byung ba'i yam shing nyid/ /thams cad kyi ni
4a6(rgyud): bsreg blugs bya/ /gzugs la sogs pa gang byung ba/ /yam shing zhes ni rab tu grags/ /de ltar sbyin sreg bshad nas ni/ /rab tu gnas pa brjod par bya/ /sku gsung
4a7(rgyud): thugs la rtag tu ni/ /gang zhig sems ni brtan gyur pa/ /de nyid rab tu gnas par brjod/ /phung po rnams kyi dngos po ci/ /gang zhig sngags kyi mtshan nyid ni/ /
4b1(rgyud): de ni gsal bar brjod par bya/ /yid rnams kyis ni skad du yang / /gang zhig gsang ba bdag gis brjod/ /skye ba med cing snang med pa/ /mtshan gzhi mtshan nyid rnam par spangs
4b2(rgyud): gsang ba'i don ni rtogs pa'i phyir/ /'di ni nga yis sngags su gsungs/ /sngags ni gsal bar bshad nas ni/ /lha rnams yang ni brjod par bya/ /phung po khams dang skye mched
4b3(rgyud): kyi| |rang bzhin gyi ni legs gnas gang / /yang dag byang chub thar pa nyid/ /de kun yang dag rab brtags shing / /gal te sems kyis nyer brtags gang / /lha zhes bya bar yang dag
4b4(rgyud): bshad/ /sku gsung thugs kyi phyag rgya las/ /de nyid du ni yang dag gsungs/ /lha la gsol btab rnal 'byor ni/ /gsal bar nga yis brjod par bya/ /de nas skyil krung bcas
4b5(rgyud): nas ni/ /sna yi rtse mor bltas nas kyang / /rang gi rang bzhin rnal 'byor gyis/ /de nyid mthong bar bzhag par bya/ /snying ga'i gnas su lag pa gnyis/ /'bad pas mnyam
4b6(rgyud): par sbyar nas su/ /mi rtog pa yi rang bzhin du/ /gang tshe sems ni rab rgyu ba/ /sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa'i bdag /de tshe de la skye bar 'gyur/ /sangs rgyas thams
4b7(rgyud): cad 'dus pa'i bdag / myur bar byin gyis rlob par 'gyur/ /sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa'i bdag /sangs rgyas kun gyi sdom pa'i bdag /thugs kyi rdo rjes gsungs pa
5a1(rgyud): @#/ /bzhin/ /rnal 'byor sangs rgyas thams cad 'gyur/ /nga yis gsal bar brjod pa ni/ /sku gsung thugs kyi grub sbyin pa/ /sangs rgyas kun mchog
5a2(rgyud): gsang ba'i don/ /thabs dang shes rab spyod yul don/ /sems can don du snying rje che/ /sangs rgyas byang chub rab sgrub pa/ /sna rtse'i dkyil 'khor nga yis gsungs/ /de dag
5a3(rgyud): thams cad dbyibs tsam du/ /mdor bsdus thams cad ma byas so/ /res 'ga' dam tshig 'khor lo yang / /de nyid zhes bya ma gsungs so/ /rtogs pa cung zad tsam gyis ni//
5a4(rgyud): gang 'grub de ni res 'ga' yang / /gsung gi 'khor lor gsungs pa yin/ /rnam rtog med par lhag mos pas/ /sgrub po dam pas bsgrub par bya/ /khrag dang khu ba de bzhin
5a5(rgyud): sha| bshang ba dang ni gci ba nyid/ /dam tshig ces bya rab 'bad par/ /gang zhig bdag gis tshig gsungs pa/ /de rnams kun la de bzhin gshegs/ /de rnams tha
5a6(rgyud): snyad tsam gyis gnas/ /gang tshe dam chig 'dod chags sems/ /des ni de nyid rab tu spyod/ /gang tshe sems ni chags gyur pa/ /de ni sems can yod ma yin/ /de la kun
5a7(rgyud): tu rtog pa yi/ /khrag ni za bar 'gyur ba'o/ /khrag ni chen po zos nas ni/ /'od dpag med pa'ang bza' bar bya/ /gang zhig chos rnams las skyes pa/ /khu ba'i sgrar ni bsgrag
5b1(rgyud): par bya/ /de tshe ma skyes rtogs pa'i phyir/ /bza' bar yang dag gsungs pa nyid/ /dngos po kun gyi mnyam pa nyid/ /sha chen du ni rab tu dbye/ /mi dmigs pa yi rnal 'byor gyis/ /
5b2(rgyud): bza' ba zhes byar mngon par brjod/ /gang zhig rab tu 'dzag pa'i sems/ /nus pa'i rjes su sbyor ba las/ /phyag rgya las kyi sbyor ba yis/ /de yang gci ba'i sgra yis brjod/ /chos
5b3(rgyud): dang chos min nges pa'i sems/ /sbas pa'i char ni gnas pa 'di/ /chos rnams thams cad rab rtogs pa'o/ /bshang ba za bar yang dag brjod/ /dam tshig nyid kyi mtshan nyid
5b4(rgyud): ni| |'di rnams thams cad gsal bar bshad/ /'di rnams don ni rtogs pa yis/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid 'gyur/ /dpal bde ba dam pa rtogs par byed pa dang ldan pa zhes
5b5(rgyud): bya ba'i rgyud byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa chen po mkha' 'gro ma dra ba sdom pa'i brtag pa rnyog pa med pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ / //rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta ga ya d+ha
5b6(rgyud): ra dang / bod kyi lo ts+tsha ba dge slong shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur ba'o// //rgya gar skad du/ shrI bud+d+ha ka pA la nA ma yo gi nI tan+t+ra rA dza/ bod skad du dpal sangs rgyas thod
5b7(rgyud): pa zhes bya ba rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ /dpal sangs rgyas thod pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
6a1(rgyud): @#/ /thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor chen po rgyan dang ldan pa'i dbus su/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / rnal
6a2(rgyud): 'byor ma rnams dang lhan cig tu bzhugs te/ 'phags pa kun dga' bo la sogs pa 'dod chags dang bral ba'i gtso bo rnams dang / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang
6a3(rgyud): phyug la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' bye ba phrag brgyad cu dang yang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis rdo rje'i tshig gis rdo rje chen po'i
6a4(rgyud): gnas su/ rgyud thams cad dang / sngags yang dag par bshad nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos rdo rje dang / pad+mo yang dag par sbyar bas btsun mo'i
6a5(rgyud): b+ha gar yongs su mya ngan las 'das so/ /de yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa mthong nas/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang / rnal 'byor ma thams cad rmad du gyur te
6a6(rgyud): gcig la gcig lta zhing / e ma'o/ /bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po dkyil 'khor chen po rgyan dang ldan pa'i dbus su ji ltar yongs su
6a7(rgyud): mya ngan las 'das/ de nas rnal 'byor ma sna tshogs sde ma la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes 'di skad ces gsol to/ /lha mo/ sems can
6b1(rgyud): bsod nams dman pa rnams nus pa la zhon par 'gyur ba'i thabs cung zad mchis sam/ gsungs pa/ rnal 'byor gyi rgyud la bye ba phrag drug nyid do/ /rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud la ni
6b2(rgyud): bye ba phrag bcu drug nyid do/ /mdo sde so so la ni bye ba phrag brgyad cu'o/ /de bzhin du pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa ni bye ba la bsgres pa'i 'bum phrag lnga'o/ /'di dag thams cad ni thub
6b3(rgyud): pa'i dbang pos gsungs so/ /sngags dang bral na ni rgyud kyis nus pa mi snang ste rgyud la lar ni ci nas sngags bye ba bzlas par gsungs so/ /bsod nams 'bring po rnams kyis ni
6b4(rgyud): sngags 'bum bzlas pas myur bar 'grub par gsungs so/ /bsod nams che bas khri bzlas pas shin tu myur bar 'grub bo/ /de ltar rdo rje can chen po rgyud kyi bdag po'i gtso bos
6b5(rgyud): gsungs so/ /bsod nams chung ba'i sems can rnams kyis ni bye ba bzlas par gsungs so/ /sems can 'bad rtsol chung ba rnams kyis ni 'bum bzlas par bdag smra'o/ /
6b6(rgyud): sems can sgom pa la zhan pa rnams kyis ni khri kho na bzlas par bya'o/ /sems can 'dod chags la zhugs pa rnams kyi bzlas pa ji ltar lags/ blun po dang / lkugs pa'i
6b7(rgyud): rigs can rnams kyi sngags kyi grangs ji ltar lags/ shin tu dmigs pa'i sngags kyis bzlas pa ji ltar lags/ 'di ltar phan tshun smra bas bzlas na dngos grub gzhan
7a1(rgyud): @#/ /du'ang 'gyur ro/ /gal te dman pa'i sems kyis nyon mongs bzhin pas bzlas pa de'i tshe bskal pa skar ma lta bur bye bar yang de la dngos grub med do//
7a2(rgyud): de ltar thos nas rnal 'byor ma sna tshogs sde ma bcom ldan 'das kyis zhal la lta bar byed cing zur mig dang bcas pa'i chags pas bltas te shin tu khro bas 'jigs par
7a3(rgyud): byed cing snying rje'i thugs 'khrugs pas bdud kyi dpung rab tu bcom mo/ /de ltar bzhugs pa'i lha mo chen mo rgyud thams cad kyi bdag po'i dbang phyug la de nas des gzigs
7a4(rgyud): pa tsam gyis bcom ldan 'das kyis dbu las sngags phyung ngo / /oM bud+d+he sid+d+he su sid+d+he/ a mr-i ta a ra dze bud+d+ha ka pA la s+phoT ne s+phoT ya trA sa ya ho hUM phaT/ de ltar sngags kyi mchog
7a5(rgyud): son pas sa rim pa bdun gyi 'og tu chud pa'i klu rnams bcom par byas shing phye mar byas nas slar 'ongs te sna tshogs sde ma'i zhal du zhugs te/ pad+ma'i nang nas byung nas
7a6(rgyud): slar thod par zhugs so/ /sngags 'di'i mthus klu rnams zhig ste/ skrag cing rdul byung bar 'gyur ro/ /nor rgyas la sogs pa'i rdzu 'phrul chen po'i klu thams cad lhags
7a7(rgyud): te| stobs kyi rgyu dang / dung skyong dang / 'jog po dang / mtha' yas dang / pad+ma chen po la sogs pa klu chen po rnams dang / gzhan gang yang rung ba dug las byung ba thams
7b1(rgyud): cad kyang lhags so/ /rnal 'byor ma sna tshogs sde ma la kha phyogs te klu thams cad kyis zhus pa/ lha mo/ bka' stsol ci zhig bgyi zhes smra'o/ /gsungs pa/ gang yang sangs rgyas
7b2(rgyud): nyams su myong ba de ltar gyis shig / de ltar thos pa tsam gyis dkyil 'khor chen po rgyan dang ldan pa'i dbus su bcom ldan 'das kyis thod pa kha phye ste glegs bam byung ngo / /
7b3(rgyud): nam mkha' la sgra byung ngo / /lha mo sna tshogs sde ma zungs/ /sems can kun la phan 'dogs ma/ /rgyud 'di rgyal po chen po ste/ /rnal 'byor ma yi gong na med/ /sangs rgyas
7b4(rgyud): thong pa zhes bya ba/ /sems can kun la phan byed pa'o/ /de ltar thos nas sna tshogs sde mas glegs bam yang dag par bzung ste/ phyag na rdo rje la nye bar btad do/ /phyag na rdo
7b5(rgyud): rjes rgyud 'di zungs/ /sems can kun la bde 'bab pa/ /rnal 'byor ma yi dngos grub kun/ /'bras bu myur du ster byed pa'o/ /mnan dang spar ba ye shes che/ /gong na med pa
7b6(rgyud): rnyed dka' ba/ /gsang ba mchog gi nyams dga' ba/ /lus kun la ni rnam par gnas/ /nam mkha' lding dang char dbab dang / /dngul chu bcud kyis len pa dang / /bskrad
7b7(rgyud): dang dbang du bya nyid dang / /rmongs dang mngon spyod nyid dang ni/ /dpung la sogs pa rengs nyid dang / /dus su zin pa bzlog pa dang / /phur bus gdab dang bsad pa dang / /rtag
8a1(rgyud): @#/ /tu sgrub pa byed pa dang / /sna tshogs sngags rim ji bzhin dang / /ji bzhin rnal 'byor ma bskyed dang / /dpal chen he ru ka yi ni/ /dus su zin pa
8a2(rgyud): bzlog pa dang / /bskyed pa dang ni gnas rgyu dang / /dngos dang dngos med spros med dang / /srid par spyod cing dgos med dang / /dgongs pas bshad pa mchog chen dang / /
8a3(rgyud): rnal 'byor ma yi mchog chen dang / /rnal 'byor ma yi 'dus pa dang / /nus pa rnam pa mang gsungs pa/ /thos pa tsam gyis 'grub par 'gyur/ /gzugs brnyan dag pa nyid dang
8a4(rgyud): ni| |de bzhin bstan pa skyong ba dang / /dur khrod 'jigs pa che bzang dang / /ro langs sgrub pa la sogs dang / /stobs po che rnams dgug pa dang / /de bzhin 'jig rten
8a5(rgyud): gsum dgug dang / /rim gyis gdung ba 'jig rten dang / /dgra yi kha sogs bcing ba dang / /de bzhin bsad dang bslu ba dang / /mi snang byed pa mchog dang ni/ /mig sman
8a6(rgyud): dang ni ril bu nyid/ /bcud len ral gri nyid dang ni/ /sangs rgyas thod pa'i sbyor ba yis/ /thos pa tsam gyis 'grub par 'gyur/ /mi snang ba ni mchog chen dang / /sna tshogs
8a7(rgyud): sgyu 'phrul rnam 'phrul dang / /rang gi gzugs ni bsgyur ba dang / /gzhan gyi lus la gzhug sogs dang / /sangs rgyas bye bas rab bsrungs pa'i/ /sangs rgyas bu mo mchog
8b1(rgyud): chen rnams/ /khros pa tsam gyis 'gugs byed na/ /gzhan dag smos lta ci zhig dgos/ /mig 'phrul byed pa nyid dang ni/ /dge mtshan rnam pa mang shes pa/ /'dod pa lnga ni bsten bzhin
8b2(rgyud): pas| |'di ru 'grub pa gdon mi za/ /'jigs shing 'joms pa'i rtsod chen po/ /gcig gis 'bum las rgyal bar byed/ /skyes pa gcig gis 'dod chen gyis/ /bud med 'bum
8b3(rgyud): phrag 'jig byed cing / /rdo rjer byed pa rnyed dga' ba/ /gcig gis thams cad 'dod pa spyad/ /de nas gzhan yang rab bshad pa/ /mkha' lding sbyor ba rim ji bzhin/ /rgyud kun du
8b4(rgyud): yang rnyed dka' ba/ /mu stegs rnams kyi yul min pa/ /rgyud kun du yang ma gsungs so/ /sangs rgyas thod pa'i gzhung ji bzhin/ /rdo rje mgon pos gsungs pa yi/ /mkha' lding
8b5(rgyud): shin tu rmad byung ba/ /'jig rten gsum na rnyed dka' ba'i/ /sbyor ba rnam pa bco brgyad gsungs/ /sha li ka yi sbyor ba dang / /rig pa 'dzin dang rgyan po 'gyed/ /rnga rdung bud med
8b6(rgyud): 'phrog pa dang / /shin bsnun zhags pas 'ching ba dang / /khu byug pad+mas 'byed pa dang / /stag byed chu blugs dung 'bud dang / /thod lo kor 'phrog skyug pa dang / /ras g.yog
8b7(rgyud): thal lcags brdab pa dang / /yig gsum bsam gtan gyis ni gtam/ /'di rnams kyis ni dgug par bya/ /mkha' lding sbyor ba bco brgyad po/ /'jig rten gsum na rab
9a1(rgyud): @#/ /rnyed dka'/ /sems can rnams la phan byed pa/ /rdo rje mgon po nyid kyis gsungs/ /de nas gzhan yang rab bshad pa/ /mchog gi ye shes ji
9a2(rgyud): bzhin pa/ /b+ha ga'i dbus su rnam par bzhugs/ /bde ba chen po ster byed pa/ /'di nyid du ni kun gnas kyang / /byis pa rmongs pas mi shes so/ /der ni bcud dang bcud
9a3(rgyud): len te/ /de nyid du ni sangs rgyas bzhugs/ /der ni dkyil 'khor bzang po'o/ /der ni slob ma dbang bskur ba'o/ /der ni he ru ka dpa' bo/ /nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i dbang gtso bo/ /der
9a4(rgyud): ni nam mkha' lding 'jigs pa/ /de nyid du ni ro langs sgrub/ /der ni dur khrod brgyad po rnams/ /skad cig tsam gyis bskyed pa'i rgyu/ /der ni sangs rgyas bdag nyid de/ /
9a5(rgyud): stong phrag gsum ni rnam par bzhugs/ /der ni 'jig rten khams kun te/ /de nyid bcom ldan 'das lha mo/ /sangs rgyas la sogs bskyed pa'i yum/ /byang chub
9a6(rgyud): sems dpa' dpal chen po/ /shes rab pha rol phyin dpung gnyen/ /de nyid bsod nams kun ster ma/ /de nyid thar pa ster byed ma/ /phyag rgya chen po grags chen
9a7(rgyud): po| |dngos grub kun ni 'dod byed ma/ /ma dang tshangs mo sring mo dang / /bu mo bud med rab brtan ma/ /shes rab mnyes shing 'jigs byed ma/ /'gro drug bde sdug
9b1(rgyud): bag chags bcas/ /'khor ba mya ngan 'das nyid dang / /bdag nyid chen po de nyid de/ /rnam rtog kun tu rtog pa nyid/ /de bzhin 'char dang nub pa dang / /nyin mtshan mal
9b2(rgyud): stan bza' ba dang / /nges pa'i brtul zhugs rtsis dang grangs/ /rnam par mi rtog yang dag rtog /dman dang mchog dang bar ma dang / /gzhan dang gang dang de dang ni/ /
9b3(rgyud): de nyid bdag nyid chen po gcig/ /sems can kun la bde ba 'bab/ /de ltar thos nas phyag na rdo rje la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang / 'dod can ma la
